layout: lexeme

###  Välipohja₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Välipohja* (middle bottom)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  10
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
